I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Bad chunked encoding should cause 400 error, not 503
### Expected Behavior

Bad chunked encoding should cause a 400 error.

### Current Behavior

The [test for VSV16](https://github.com/varnishcache/varnish-cache/blob/7d6cfa384d7296646e73c80e572fbe182274d701/bin/varnishtest/tests/f00016.vtc) shows that malformed chunked responses cause a 503 error, which is clearly wrong.

### Possible Solution

Varnish should differentiate between “failed to parse data from client” and “failed to fetch response from backend”.  It appears that it is the conflation of the two that causes the error.

### Steps to Reproduce (for bugs)

Run `make -C bin/varnishtest check-TESTS TESTS=tests/f00016.vtc` and notice that the tests passes with the 503 status codes.

### Context

This is almost certainly quite minor, as only buggy or malicious clients can trigger this code path.  Correct clients will not be affected, and setups where Varnish is behind NGINX or HAProxy (as a layer 7 reverse proxy) will not be affected either.

### Varnish Cache version

 varnishd (varnish-trunk revision 7d6cfa384d7296646e73c80e572fbe182274d701)

### Operating system

Fedora 41 with Linux 6.12.25

### Source of binary packages used (if any)

None

</pr_description>

    26	 * HOWEVER CAUSED AND ON ANY THEORY OF LIABILITY, WHETHER IN CONTRACT, STRICT
    27	 * LIABILITY, OR TORT (INCLUDING NEGLIGENCE OR OTHERWISE) ARISING IN ANY WAY
    28	 * OUT OF THE USE OF THIS SOFTWARE, EVEN IF ADVISED OF THE POSSIBILITY OF
    29	 * SUCH DAMAGE.
    30	 *
    31	 * HTTP1 Fetch Filters
    32	 *
    33	 * These filters are used for both req.body and beresp.body to handle
    34	 * the HTTP/1 aspects (C-L/Chunked/EOF)
    35	 *
    36	 */
    37	
    38	#include "config.h"
    39	
    40	#include <inttypes.h>
    41	
    42	#include "cache/cache_varnishd.h"
    43	#include "cache/cache_filter.h"
    44	#include "cache_http1.h"
    45	
    46	#include "vct.h"
    47	#include "vtcp.h"
    48	
    49	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
    50	 * Read up to len bytes, returning pipelined data first.
    51	 */
    52	
    53	static ssize_t
    54	v1f_read(const struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct http_conn *htc, void *d, ssize_t len)
    55	{
    56	        ssize_t l;
    57	        unsigned char *p;
    58	        ssize_t i = 0;
    59	
    60	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
    61	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(htc, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
    62	        assert(len > 0);
    63	        l = 0;
    64	        p = d;
    65	        if (htc->pipeline_b) {
    66	                l = htc->pipeline_e - htc->pipeline_b;
    67	                assert(l > 0);
    68	                l = vmin(l, len);
    69	                memcpy(p, htc->pipeline_b, l);
    70	                p += l;
    71	                len -= l;
    72	                htc->pipeline_b += l;
    73	                if (htc->pipeline_b == htc->pipeline_e)
    74	                        htc->pipeline_b = htc->pipeline_e = NULL;
    75	        }
    76	        if (len > 0) {
    77	                i = read(*htc->rfd, p, len);
    78	                if (i < 0) {
    79	                        VTCP_Assert(i);
    80	                        VSLbs(vc->wrk->vsl, SLT_FetchError,
    81	                            TOSTRAND(VAS_errtxt(errno)));
    82	                        return (i);
    83	                }
    84	                assert(i <= len);
    85	                if (i == 0)
    86	                        htc->doclose = SC_RESP_CLOSE;
    87	        }
    88	        assert(i >= 0);
    89	        assert(l >= 0);
    90	        assert(i < SSIZE_MAX / 2);
    91	        assert(l < SSIZE_MAX / 2);
    92	        return (i + l);
    93	}
    94	
    95	
    96	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
    97	 * read (CR)?LF at the end of a chunk
    98	 */
    99	static enum vfp_status
   100	v1f_chunk_end(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct http_conn *htc)
   101	{
   102	        char c;
   103	
   104	        if (v1f_read(vc, htc, &c, 1) <= 0)
   105	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked read err"));
   106	        if (c == '\r' && v1f_read(vc, htc, &c, 1) <= 0)
   107	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked read err"));
   108	        if (c != '\n')
   109	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked tail no NL"));
   110	        return (VFP_OK);
   111	}
   112	
   113	
   114	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
   115	 * Parse a chunk header and, for VFP_OK, return size in a pointer
   116	 *
   117	 * XXX: Reading one byte at a time is pretty pessimal.
   118	 */
   119	
   120	static enum vfp_status
   121	v1f_chunked_hdr(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct http_conn *htc, ssize_t *szp)
   122	{
   123	        char buf[20];           /* XXX: 20 is arbitrary */
   124	        unsigned u;
   125	        uintmax_t cll;
   126	        ssize_t cl, lr;
   127	        char *q;
   128	
   129	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   130	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(htc, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
   131	        AN(szp);
   132	        assert(*szp == -1);
   133	
   134	        /* Skip leading whitespace */
   135	        do {
   136	                lr = v1f_read(vc, htc, buf, 1);
   137	                if (lr <= 0)
   138	                        return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked read err"));
   139	        } while (vct_isows(buf[0]));
   140	
   141	        if (!vct_ishex(buf[0]))
   142	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked header non-hex"));
   143	
   144	        /* Collect hex digits, skipping leading zeros */
   145	        for (u = 1; u < sizeof buf; u++) {
   146	                do {
   147	                        lr = v1f_read(vc, htc, buf + u, 1);
   148	                        if (lr <= 0)
   149	                                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked read err"));
   150	                } while (u == 1 && buf[0] == '0' && buf[u] == '0');
   151	                if (!vct_ishex(buf[u]))
   152	                        break;
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        if (u >= sizeof buf)
   156	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked header too long"));
   157	
   158	        /* Skip trailing white space */
   159	        while (vct_isows(buf[u])) {
   160	                lr = v1f_read(vc, htc, buf + u, 1);
   161	                if (lr <= 0)
   162	                        return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked read err"));
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        if (buf[u] == '\r' && v1f_read(vc, htc, buf + u, 1) <= 0)
   166	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked read err"));
   167	        if (buf[u] != '\n')
   168	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked header no NL"));
   169	
   170	        buf[u] = '\0';
   171	
   172	        cll = strtoumax(buf, &q, 16);
   173	        if (q == NULL || *q != '\0')
   174	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked header number syntax"));
   175	        cl = (ssize_t)cll;
   176	        if (cl < 0 || (uintmax_t)cl != cll)
   177	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "bogusly large chunk size"));
   178	
   179	        *szp = cl;
   180	        return (VFP_OK);
   181	}
   182	
   183	
   184	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
   185	 * Read a chunked HTTP object.
   186	 *
   187	 */
   188	
   189	static enum vfp_status v_matchproto_(vfp_pull_f)
   190	v1f_chunked_pull(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct vfp_entry *vfe, void *ptr,
   191	    ssize_t *lp)
   192	{
   193	        static enum vfp_status vfps;
   194	        struct http_conn *htc;
   195	        ssize_t l, lr;
   196	
   197	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   198	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vfe, VFP_ENTRY_MAGIC);
   199	        CAST_OBJ_NOTNULL(htc, vfe->priv1, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
   200	        AN(ptr);
   201	        AN(lp);
   202	
   203	        l = *lp;
   204	        *lp = 0;
   205	        if (vfe->priv2 == -1) {
   206	                vfps = v1f_chunked_hdr(vc, htc, &vfe->priv2);
   207	                if (vfps != VFP_OK)
   208	                        return (vfps);
   209	        }
   210	        if (vfe->priv2 > 0) {
   211	                if (vfe->priv2 < l)
   212	                        l = vfe->priv2;
   213	                lr = v1f_read(vc, htc, ptr, l);
   214	                if (lr <= 0)
   215	                        return (VFP_Error(vc, "chunked insufficient bytes"));
   216	                *lp = lr;
   217	                vfe->priv2 -= lr;
   218	                if (vfe->priv2 != 0)
   219	                        return (VFP_OK);
   220	
   221	                vfe->priv2 = -1;
   222	                return (v1f_chunk_end(vc, htc));
   223	        }
   224	        AZ(vfe->priv2);
   225	        vfps = v1f_chunk_end(vc, htc);
   226	        return (vfps == VFP_OK ? VFP_END : vfps);
   227	}
   228	
   229	static const struct vfp v1f_chunked = {
   230	        .name = "V1F_CHUNKED",
   231	        .pull = v1f_chunked_pull,
   232	};
   233	
   234	
   235	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   236	
   237	static enum vfp_status v_matchproto_(vfp_pull_f)
   238	v1f_straight_pull(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct vfp_entry *vfe, void *p,
   239	    ssize_t *lp)
   240	{
   241	        ssize_t l, lr;
   242	        struct http_conn *htc;
   243	
   244	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   245	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vfe, VFP_ENTRY_MAGIC);
   246	        CAST_OBJ_NOTNULL(htc, vfe->priv1, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
   247	        AN(p);
   248	        AN(lp);
   249	
   250	        l = *lp;
   251	        *lp = 0;
   252	
   253	        if (vfe->priv2 == 0) // XXX: Optimize Content-Len: 0 out earlier
   254	                return (VFP_END);
   255	        l = vmin(l, vfe->priv2);
   256	        lr = v1f_read(vc, htc, p, l);
   257	        if (lr <= 0)
   258	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "straight insufficient bytes"));
   259	        *lp = lr;
   260	        vfe->priv2 -= lr;
   261	        if (vfe->priv2 == 0)
   262	                return (VFP_END);
   263	        return (VFP_OK);
   264	}
   265	
   266	static const struct vfp v1f_straight = {
   267	        .name = "V1F_STRAIGHT",
   268	        .pull = v1f_straight_pull,
   269	};
   270	
   271	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   272	
   273	static enum vfp_status v_matchproto_(vfp_pull_f)
   274	v1f_eof_pull(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct vfp_entry *vfe, void *p, ssize_t *lp)
   275	{
   276	        ssize_t l, lr;
   277	        struct http_conn *htc;
   278	
   279	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   280	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vfe, VFP_ENTRY_MAGIC);
   281	        CAST_OBJ_NOTNULL(htc, vfe->priv1, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
   282	        AN(p);
   283	
   284	        AN(lp);
   285	
   286	        l = *lp;
   287	        *lp = 0;
   288	        lr = v1f_read(vc, htc, p, l);
   289	        if (lr < 0)
   290	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "eof socket fail"));
   291	        if (lr == 0)
   292	                return (VFP_END);
   293	        *lp = lr;
   294	        return (VFP_OK);
   295	}
   296	
   297	static const struct vfp v1f_eof = {
   298	        .name = "V1F_EOF",
   299	        .pull = v1f_eof_pull,
   300	};
   301	
   302	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
   303	 */
   304	
   305	int
   306	V1F_Setup_Fetch(struct vfp_ctx *vfc, struct http_conn *htc)
   307	{
   308	        struct vfp_entry *vfe;
   309	
   310	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vfc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   311	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(htc, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
   312	
   313	        if (htc->body_status == BS_EOF) {
   314	                assert(htc->content_length == -1);
   315	                vfe = VFP_Push(vfc, &v1f_eof);
   316	                if (vfe == NULL)
   317	                        return (ENOSPC);
   318	                vfe->priv2 = 0;
   319	        } else if (htc->body_status == BS_LENGTH) {
   320	                assert(htc->content_length > 0);
   321	                vfe = VFP_Push(vfc, &v1f_straight);
   322	                if (vfe == NULL)
   323	                        return (ENOSPC);
   324	                vfe->priv2 = htc->content_length;
   325	        } else if (htc->body_status == BS_CHUNKED) {
   326	                assert(htc->content_length == -1);
   327	                vfe = VFP_Push(vfc, &v1f_chunked);
   328	                if (vfe == NULL)
   329	                        return (ENOSPC);
   330	                vfe->priv2 = -1;
   331	        } else {
   332	                WRONG("Wrong body_status");
   333	        }
   334	        vfe->priv1 = htc;
   335	        return (0);
   336	}
   337

   108	        VDP_NULL,               /* Input buffer valid after call */
   109	        VDP_FLUSH,              /* Input buffer will be invalidated */

   114	typedef int vdp_init_f(VRT_CTX, struct vdp_ctx *, void **priv);
   115	/*
   116	 * Return value:
   117	 *      negative:       Error - abandon delivery
   118	 *      zero:           OK
   119	 *      positive:       Don't push this VDP anyway
   120	 */
   121	
   122	typedef int vdp_fini_f(struct vdp_ctx *, void **priv);
   123	typedef int vdp_bytes_f(struct vdp_ctx *, enum vdp_action, void **priv,
   124	    const void *ptr, ssize_t len);
   125	
   126	/*
   127	 * ============================================================
   128	 * vdpio io-vector interface
   129	 */
   130	typedef int vdpio_init_f(VRT_CTX, struct vdp_ctx *, void **priv, int capacity);
   131	/*
   132	 * the vdpio_init_f() are called front (object iterator) to back (consumer).
   133	 *
   134	 * each init function returns the minimum number of io vectors (vscarab
   135	 * capacity) that it requires the next filter to accept. This capacity is
   136	 * passed to the next init function such that it can allocate sufficient
   137	 * space to fulfil the requirement of the previous filter.
   138	 *
   139	 * Return values:
   140	 *   < 0 : Error
   141	 *  == 0 ; NOOP, do not push this filter
   142	 *  >= 1 : capacity requirement
   143	 *
   144	 * typedef is shared with upgrade
   145	 */
   146	
   147	typedef int vdpio_lease_f(struct vdp_ctx *, struct vdp_entry *, struct vscarab *scarab);
   148	/*
   149	 * vdpio_lease_f() returns leases provided by this filter layer in the vscarab
   150	 * probided by the caller.
   151	 *
   152	 * called via vdpio_pull(): the last filter is called first by delivery. Each
   153	 * filter calls the previous layer for leases. The first filter calls storage.
   154	 *
   155	 * return values are as for ObjVAIlease()
   156	 *
   157	 * Other notable differences to vdp_bytes_f:
   158	 * - responsible for updating (struct vdp_entry).bytes_in and .calls
   159	 *
   160	 */
   161	
   162	typedef void vdpio_fini_f(struct vdp_ctx *, void **priv);
   163

   208	
   209	int VDP_bytes(struct vdp_ctx *, enum vdp_action act, const void *, ssize_t);
   210	
   211	/*
   212	 * vdpe == NULL: get lesaes from the last layer
   213	 * vdpe != NULL: get leases from the previous layer or storage
   214	 *
   215	 * conversely to VDP_bytes, vdpio calls happen back (delivery) to front (storage)
   216	 *
   217	 * ends up in a tail call to the previous layer to save stack space
   218	 */
   219	static inline int
   220	vdpio_pull(struct vdp_ctx *vdc, struct vdp_entry *vdpe, struct vscarab *scarab)
   221	{
   222	
   223	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vdc, VDP_CTX_MAGIC);
   224	
   225	        if (vdpe == NULL)
   226	                vdpe = VTAILQ_LAST(&vdc->vdp, vdp_entry_s);
   227	        else {
   228	                CHECK_OBJ(vdpe, VDP_ENTRY_MAGIC);
   229	                vdpe = VTAILQ_PREV(vdpe, vdp_entry_s, list);
   230	        }
   231	
   232	        if (vdpe != NULL)
   233	                return (vdpe->vdp->io_lease(vdc, vdpe, scarab));
   234	        else
   235	                return (ObjVAIlease(vdc->wrk, vdc->vai_hdl, scarab));
   236	}
   237	
   238	uint64_t VDPIO_Close1(struct vdp_ctx *, struct vdp_entry *vdpe);
   239	
   240	/*
   241	 * ============================================================
   242	 * VDPIO helpers
   243	 */
   244	
   245	/*
   246	 * l bytes have been written to buf. save these to out and checkpoint buf for
   247	 * the remaining free space
   248	 */
   249	static inline void
   250	iovec_collect(struct iovec *buf, struct iovec *out, size_t l)
   251	{
   252	        if (out->iov_base == NULL)
   253	                out->iov_base = buf->iov_base;
   254	        assert((char *)out->iov_base + out->iov_len == buf->iov_base);
   255	        out->iov_len += l;
   256	        buf->iov_base = (char *)buf->iov_base + l;
   257	        buf->iov_len -= l;
   258	}
   259	
   260	/*
   261	 * return a single lease via the vdc vscaret
   262	 */
   263	static inline
   264	void vdpio_return_lease(const struct vdp_ctx *vdc, uint64_t lease)
   265	{
   266	        struct vscaret *scaret;
   267	
   268	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vdc, VDP_CTX_MAGIC);
   269	        scaret = vdc->scaret;
   270	        VSCARET_CHECK_NOTNULL(scaret);
   271	
   272	        if (scaret->used == scaret->capacity)
   273	                ObjVAIreturn(vdc->wrk, vdc->vai_hdl, scaret);
   274	        VSCARET_ADD(scaret, lease);
   275	}
   276	
   277	/*
   278	 * add all leases from the vscarab to the vscaret
   279	 */
   280	static inline
   281	void vdpio_return_vscarab(const struct vdp_ctx *vdc, struct vscarab *scarab)
   282	{
   283	        struct viov *v;
   284	
   285	        VSCARAB_CHECK_NOTNULL(scarab);
   286	        VSCARAB_FOREACH(v, scarab)
   287	                vdpio_return_lease(vdc, v->lease);
   288	        AZ(v);
   289	        VSCARAB_INIT(scarab, scarab->capacity);
   290	}
   291	
   292	/*
   293	 * return used up iovs (len == 0)
   294	 * move remaining to the beginning of the scarab
   295	 */
   296	static inline void
   297	vdpio_consolidate_vscarab(const struct vdp_ctx *vdc, struct vscarab *scarab)
   298	{
   299	        struct viov *v, *f = NULL;
   300	
   301	        VSCARAB_CHECK_NOTNULL(scarab);
   302	        VSCARAB_FOREACH(v, scarab) {
   303	                if (v->iov.iov_len == 0) {
   304	                        AN(v->iov.iov_base);
   305	                        vdpio_return_lease(vdc, v->lease);
   306	                        if (f == NULL)
   307	                                f = v;
   308	                        continue;
   309	                }
   310	                else if (f == NULL)
   311	                        continue;
   312	                memmove(f, v, scarab->used - (v - scarab->s) * sizeof (*v));
   313	                break;
   314	        }
   315	        if (f != NULL)
   316	                scarab->used = f - scarab->s;
   317	}

   320	int VDPIO_Init(struct vdp_ctx *vdc, struct objcore *oc, struct ws *ws,
   321	    vai_notify_cb *notify_cb, void *notify_priv, struct vscaret *scaret);
   322	void VDPIO_Return(const struct vdp_ctx *vdc);
   323	void VDPIO_Fini(struct vdp_ctx *vdc);

    40	static unsigned fetchfrag;
    41	
    42	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
    43	 * We want to issue the first error we encounter on fetching and
    44	 * suppress the rest.  This function does that.
    45	 *
    46	 * Other code is allowed to look at busyobj->fetch_failed to bail out
    47	 *
    48	 * For convenience, always return VFP_ERROR
    49	 */
    50	
    51	enum vfp_status
    52	VFP_Error(struct vfp_ctx *vc, const char *fmt, ...)
    53	{
    54	        va_list ap;
    55	
    56	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
    57	        if (!vc->failed) {
    58	                va_start(ap, fmt);
    59	                VSLbv(vc->wrk->vsl, SLT_FetchError, fmt, ap);
    60	                va_end(ap);
    61	                vc->failed = 1;
    62	        }
    63	        return (VFP_ERROR);
    64	}
    65	
    66	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
    67	 * Fetch Storage to put object into.
    68	 *
    69	 */
    70	
    71	enum vfp_status
    72	VFP_GetStorage(struct vfp_ctx *vc, ssize_t *sz, uint8_t **ptr)
    73	{
    74	
    75	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
    76	        AN(sz);
    77	        assert(*sz >= 0);
    78	        AN(ptr);
    79	
    80	        if (fetchfrag > 0)
    81	                *sz = fetchfrag;
    82	
    83	        if (!ObjGetSpace(vc->wrk, vc->oc, sz, ptr)) {
    84	                *sz = 0;
    85	                *ptr = NULL;
    86	                return (VFP_Error(vc, "Could not get storage"));
    87	        }
    88	        assert(*sz > 0);
    89	        AN(*ptr);
    90	        return (VFP_OK);
    91	}
    92	
    93	void
    94	VFP_Extend(const struct vfp_ctx *vc, ssize_t sz, enum vfp_status flg)
    95	{
    96	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
    97	
    98	        ObjExtend(vc->wrk, vc->oc, sz, flg == VFP_END ? 1 : 0);
    99	}
   100	
   101	/**********************************************************************
   102	 */
   103	
   104	void
   105	VFP_Setup(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct worker *wrk)
   106	{
   107	
   108	        INIT_OBJ(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   109	        VTAILQ_INIT(&vc->vfp);
   110	        vc->wrk = wrk;
   111	}
   112	
   113	/**********************************************************************
   114	 * Returns the number of bytes processed by the lowest VFP in the stack
   115	 */
   116	
   117	uint64_t
   118	VFP_Close(struct vfp_ctx *vc)
   119	{
   120	        struct vfp_entry *vfe, *tmp;
   121	        uint64_t rv = 0;
   122	
   123	        VTAILQ_FOREACH_SAFE(vfe, &vc->vfp, list, tmp) {
   124	                if (vfe->vfp->fini != NULL)
   125	                        vfe->vfp->fini(vc, vfe);
   126	                rv = vfe->bytes_out;
   127	                VSLb(vc->wrk->vsl, SLT_VfpAcct, "%s %ju %ju", vfe->vfp->name,
   128	                    (uintmax_t)vfe->calls, (uintmax_t)rv);
   129	                VTAILQ_REMOVE(&vc->vfp, vfe, list);
   130	        }
   131	        return (rv);
   132	}
   133	
   134	int
   135	VFP_Open(VRT_CTX, struct vfp_ctx *vc)
   136	{
   137	        struct vfp_entry *vfe;
   138	
   139	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(ctx, VRT_CTX_MAGIC);
   140	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   141	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc->resp, HTTP_MAGIC);
   142	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc->wrk, WORKER_MAGIC);
   143	        AN(vc->wrk->vsl);
   144	
   145	        VTAILQ_FOREACH_REVERSE(vfe, &vc->vfp, vfp_entry_s, list) {
   146	                if (vfe->vfp->init == NULL)
   147	                        continue;
   148	                if (DO_DEBUG(DBG_PROCESSORS))
   149	                        VSLb(vc->wrk->vsl, SLT_Debug, "VFP_Open(%s)",
   150	                             vfe->vfp->name);
   151	                vfe->closed = vfe->vfp->init(ctx, vc, vfe);
   152	                if (vfe->closed != VFP_OK && vfe->closed != VFP_NULL) {
   153	                        (void)VFP_Error(vc, "Fetch filter %s failed to open",
   154	                            vfe->vfp->name);
   155	                        (void)VFP_Close(vc);
   156	                        return (-1);
   157	                }
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        return (0);
   161	}
   162	
   163	/**********************************************************************
   164	 * Suck data up from lower levels.
   165	 * Once a layer return non VFP_OK, clean it up and produce the same
   166	 * return value for any subsequent calls.
   167	 */
   168	
   169	enum vfp_status
   170	VFP_Suck(struct vfp_ctx *vc, void *p, ssize_t *lp)
   171	{
   172	        enum vfp_status vp;
   173	        struct vfp_entry *vfe, *vfe_prev;
   174	        const char *prev_name = "<storage>";
   175	        ssize_t limit;
   176	
   177	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   178	        AN(p);
   179	        AN(lp);
   180	        limit = *lp;
   181	        vfe = vc->vfp_nxt;
   182	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vfe, VFP_ENTRY_MAGIC);
   183	        vc->vfp_nxt = VTAILQ_NEXT(vfe, list);
   184	
   185	        vfe_prev = VTAILQ_PREV(vfe, vfp_entry_s, list);
   186	        if (vfe_prev != NULL)
   187	                prev_name = vfe_prev->vfp->name;
   188	
   189	        if (vfe->closed == VFP_NULL) {
   190	                /* Layer asked to be bypassed when opened */
   191	                vp = VFP_Suck(vc, p, lp);
   192	                VFP_DEBUG(vc, "bypassing %s vp=%d", vfe->vfp->name, vp);
   193	        } else if (vfe->closed == VFP_OK) {
   194	                vp = vfe->vfp->pull(vc, vfe, p, lp);
   195	                VFP_DEBUG(vc, "%s pulled %zdB/%zdB from %s vp=%d",
   196	                    prev_name, *lp, limit, vfe->vfp->name, vp);
   197	                if (vp != VFP_OK && vp != VFP_END && vp != VFP_ERROR)
   198	                        vp = VFP_Error(vc, "Fetch filter %s returned %d",
   199	                            vfe->vfp->name, vp);
   200	                else
   201	                        vfe->bytes_out += *lp;
   202	                vfe->closed = vp;
   203	                vfe->calls++;
   204	        } else {
   205	                /* Already closed filter */
   206	                *lp = 0;
   207	                vp = vfe->closed;
   208	                VFP_DEBUG(vc, "ignoring %s vp=%d", vfe->vfp->name, vp);
   209	        }
   210	        vc->vfp_nxt = vfe;
   211	        assert(vp != VFP_NULL);
   212	        return (vp);
   213	}
   214	
   215	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
   216	 */
   217	
   218	struct vfp_entry *
   219	VFP_Push(struct vfp_ctx *vc, const struct vfp *vfp)
   220	{
   221	        struct vfp_entry *vfe;
   222	
   223	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
   224	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(vc->resp, HTTP_MAGIC);
   225	
   226	        vfe = WS_Alloc(vc->resp->ws, sizeof *vfe);
   227	        if (vfe == NULL) {
   228	                (void)VFP_Error(vc, "Workspace overflow");
   229	                return (NULL);
   230	        }
   231	
   232	        INIT_OBJ(vfe, VFP_ENTRY_MAGIC);
   233	        vfe->vfp = vfp;
   234	        vfe->closed = VFP_OK;
   235	        VTAILQ_INSERT_HEAD(&vc->vfp, vfe, list);
   236	        vc->vfp_nxt = vfe;
   237	        return (vfe);
   238	}
   239	
   240	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
   241	 * Debugging aids
   242	 */
   243	
   244	static void v_matchproto_(cli_func_t)
   245	debug_fragfetch(struct cli *cli, const char * const *av, void *priv)
   246	{
   247	        (void)priv;
   248	        (void)cli;
   249	        fetchfrag = strtoul(av[2], NULL, 0);
   250	}
   251	
   252	static struct cli_proto debug_cmds[] = {
   253	        { CLICMD_DEBUG_FRAGFETCH,               "d", debug_fragfetch },
   254	        { NULL }
   255	};

   258	 *
   259	 */
   260

   262	VFP_Init(void)
   263	{
   264	
   265	        CLI_AddFuncs(debug_cmds);
   266	}

    32	
    33	#include "config.h"
    34	
    35	#include <stdlib.h>
    36	
    37	#include "cache_varnishd.h"
    38	#include "cache_filter.h"
    39	#include "cache_objhead.h"
    40	#include "cache_transport.h"
    41	
    42	#include "vtim.h"
    43	#include "storage/storage.h"
    44	
    45	/*----------------------------------------------------------------------
    46	 * Pull the req.body in via/into a objcore
    47	 *
    48	 * This can be called only once per request
    49	 *
    50	 */
    51	
    52	static ssize_t
    53	vrb_pull(struct req *req, ssize_t maxsize, objiterate_f *func, void *priv)
    54	{
    55	        ssize_t l, r = 0, yet;
    56	        struct vrt_ctx ctx[1];
    57	        struct vfp_ctx *vfc;
    58	        uint8_t *ptr;
    59	        enum vfp_status vfps = VFP_ERROR;
    60	        const struct stevedore *stv;
    61	        ssize_t req_bodybytes = 0;
    62	        unsigned flush = OBJ_ITER_FLUSH;
    63	
    64	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
    65	
    66	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req->htc, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
    67	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req->vfc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
    68	        vfc = req->vfc;
    69	
    70	        req->body_oc = HSH_Private(req->wrk);
    71	        AN(req->body_oc);
    72	
    73	        if (req->storage != NULL)
    74	                stv = req->storage;
    75	        else
    76	                stv = stv_transient;
    77	
    78	        req->storage = NULL;
    79	
    80	        if (STV_NewObject(req->wrk, req->body_oc, stv, 0) == 0) {
    81	                req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
    82	                HSH_DerefBoc(req->wrk, req->body_oc);
    83	                AZ(HSH_DerefObjCore(req->wrk, &req->body_oc, 0));
    84	                (void)VFP_Error(vfc, "Object allocation failed:"
    85	                    " Ran out of space in %s", stv->vclname);
    86	                return (-1);
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        vfc->oc = req->body_oc;
    90	
    91	        INIT_OBJ(ctx, VRT_CTX_MAGIC);
    92	        VCL_Req2Ctx(ctx, req);
    93	
    94	        if (req->vfp_filter_list != NULL &&
    95	            VCL_StackVFP(vfc, req->vcl, req->vfp_filter_list)) {
    96	                (void)VFP_Error(vfc, "req.body filters failed");
    97	                req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
    98	                HSH_DerefBoc(req->wrk, req->body_oc);
    99	                AZ(HSH_DerefObjCore(req->wrk, &req->body_oc, 0));
   100	                return (-1);
   101	        }
   102	
   103	
   104	        if (VFP_Open(ctx, vfc) < 0) {
   105	                req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
   106	                HSH_DerefBoc(req->wrk, req->body_oc);
   107	                AZ(HSH_DerefObjCore(req->wrk, &req->body_oc, 0));
   108	                return (-1);
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        AN(req->htc);
   112	        yet = req->htc->content_length;
   113	        if (yet != 0 && req->want100cont) {
   114	                req->want100cont = 0;
   115	                (void)req->transport->minimal_response(req, 100);
   116	        }
   117	        yet = vmax_t(ssize_t, yet, 0);
   118	        do {
   119	                AZ(vfc->failed);
   120	                if (maxsize >= 0 && req_bodybytes > maxsize) {
   121	                        (void)VFP_Error(vfc, "Request body too big to cache");
   122	                        break;
   123	                }
   124	                /* NB: only attempt a full allocation when caching. */
   125	                l = maxsize > 0 ? yet : 0;
   126	                if (VFP_GetStorage(vfc, &l, &ptr) != VFP_OK)
   127	                        break;
   128	                AZ(vfc->failed);
   129	                AN(ptr);
   130	                AN(l);
   131	                vfps = VFP_Suck(vfc, ptr, &l);
   132	                if (l > 0 && vfps != VFP_ERROR) {
   133	                        req_bodybytes += l;
   134	                        if (yet >= l)
   135	                                yet -= l;
   136	                        else if (yet > 0)
   137	                                yet = 0;
   138	                        if (func != NULL) {
   139	                                if (vfps == VFP_END)
   140	                                        flush |= OBJ_ITER_END;
   141	                                r = func(priv, flush, ptr, l);
   142	                                if (r)
   143	                                        break;
   144	                        } else {
   145	                                ObjExtend(req->wrk, req->body_oc, l,
   146	                                    vfps == VFP_END ? 1 : 0);
   147	                        }
   148	                }
   149	
   150	        } while (vfps == VFP_OK);
   151	        req->acct.req_bodybytes += VFP_Close(vfc);
   152	        VSLb_ts_req(req, "ReqBody", VTIM_real());
   153	        if (func != NULL) {
   154	                HSH_DerefBoc(req->wrk, req->body_oc);
   155	                AZ(HSH_DerefObjCore(req->wrk, &req->body_oc, 0));
   156	                if (vfps == VFP_END && r == 0 && (flush & OBJ_ITER_END) == 0)
   157	                        r = func(priv, flush | OBJ_ITER_END, NULL, 0);
   158	                if (vfps != VFP_END) {
   159	                        req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
   160	                        if (r == 0)
   161	                                r = -1;
   162	                }
   163	                return (r);
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        AZ(ObjSetU64(req->wrk, req->body_oc, OA_LEN, req_bodybytes));
   167	        HSH_DerefBoc(req->wrk, req->body_oc);
   168	
   169	        if (vfps != VFP_END) {
   170	                req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
   171	                AZ(HSH_DerefObjCore(req->wrk, &req->body_oc, 0));
   172	                return (-1);
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        assert(req_bodybytes >= 0);
   176	        if (req_bodybytes != req->htc->content_length) {
   177	                /* We must update also the "pristine" req.* copy */
   178	                http_Unset(req->http0, H_Content_Length);
   179	                http_Unset(req->http0, H_Transfer_Encoding);
   180	                http_PrintfHeader(req->http0, "Content-Length: %ju",
   181	                    (uintmax_t)req_bodybytes);
   182	
   183	                http_Unset(req->http, H_Content_Length);
   184	                http_Unset(req->http, H_Transfer_Encoding);
   185	                http_PrintfHeader(req->http, "Content-Length: %ju",
   186	                    (uintmax_t)req_bodybytes);
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        req->req_body_status = BS_CACHED;
   190	        return (req_bodybytes);
   191	}
   192	
   193	/*----------------------------------------------------------------------
   194	 * Iterate over the req.body.
   195	 *
   196	 * This can be done exactly once if uncached, and multiple times if the
   197	 * req.body is cached.
   198	 *
   199	 * return length or -1 on error
   200	 */
   201	
   202	ssize_t
   203	VRB_Iterate(struct worker *wrk, struct vsl_log *vsl,
   204	    struct req *req, objiterate_f *func, void *priv)
   205	{
   206	        int i;
   207	
   208	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
   209	        AN(func);
   210	
   211	        if (req->req_body_status == BS_CACHED) {
   212	                AN(req->body_oc);
   213	                if (ObjIterate(wrk, req->body_oc, priv, func, 0))
   214	                        return (-1);
   215	                return (0);
   216	        }
   217	        if (req->req_body_status == BS_NONE)
   218	                return (0);
   219	        if (req->req_body_status == BS_TAKEN) {
   220	                VSLb(vsl, SLT_VCL_Error,
   221	                    "Uncached req.body can only be consumed once.");
   222	                return (-1);
   223	        }
   224	        if (req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR) {
   225	                VSLb(vsl, SLT_FetchError,
   226	                    "Had failed reading req.body before.");
   227	                return (-1);
   228	        }
   229	        Lck_Lock(&req->sp->mtx);
   230	        if (req->req_body_status->avail > 0) {
   231	                req->req_body_status = BS_TAKEN;
   232	                i = 0;
   233	        } else
   234	                i = -1;
   235	        Lck_Unlock(&req->sp->mtx);
   236	        if (i) {
   237	                VSLb(vsl, SLT_VCL_Error,
   238	                    "Multiple attempts to access non-cached req.body");
   239	                return (i);
   240	        }
   241	        return (vrb_pull(req, -1, func, priv));
   242	}
   243	
   244	/*----------------------------------------------------------------------
   245	 * VRB_Ignore() is a dedicated function, because we might
   246	 * be able to dissuade or terminate its transmission in some protocols.
   247	 *
   248	 * For HTTP1, we do nothing if we are going to close the connection anyway or
   249	 * just iterate it into oblivion.
   250	 */
   251	
   252	static int v_matchproto_(objiterate_f)
   253	httpq_req_body_discard(void *priv, unsigned flush, const void *ptr, ssize_t len)
   254	{
   255	
   256	        (void)priv;
   257	        (void)flush;
   258	        (void)ptr;
   259	        (void)len;
   260	        return (0);
   261	}
   262	
   263	int
   264	VRB_Ignore(struct req *req)
   265	{
   266	
   267	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
   268	
   269	        if (req->doclose != SC_NULL)
   270	                return (0);
   271	        if (req->req_body_status->avail > 0)
   272	                (void)VRB_Iterate(req->wrk, req->vsl, req,
   273	                    httpq_req_body_discard, NULL);
   274	        if (req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR)
   275	                req->doclose = SC_RX_BODY;
   276	        return (0);
   277	}
   278	
   279	/*----------------------------------------------------------------------
   280	 */
   281	
   282	void
   283	VRB_Free(struct req *req)
   284	{
   285	        int r;
   286	
   287	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
   288	
   289	        if (req->body_oc == NULL)
   290	                return;
   291	
   292	        r = HSH_DerefObjCore(req->wrk, &req->body_oc, 0);
   293	
   294	        // each busyobj may have gained a reference
   295	        assert (r >= 0);
   296	        assert ((unsigned)r <= req->restarts + 1);
   297	}
   298	
   299	/*----------------------------------------------------------------------
   300	 * Cache the req.body if it is smaller than the given size
   301	 *
   302	 * This function must be called before any backend fetches are kicked
   303	 * off to prevent parallelism.
   304	 */
   305	
   306	ssize_t
   307	VRB_Cache(struct req *req, ssize_t maxsize)
   308	{
   309	        uint64_t u;
   310	
   311	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
   312	        assert (req->req_step == R_STP_RECV);
   313	        assert(maxsize >= 0);
   314	
   315	        /*
   316	         * We only allow caching to happen the first time through vcl_recv{}
   317	         * where we know we will have no competition or conflicts for the
   318	         * updates to req.http.* etc.
   319	         */
   320	        if (req->restarts > 0 && req->req_body_status != BS_CACHED) {
   321	                VSLb(req->vsl, SLT_VCL_Error,
   322	                    "req.body must be cached before restarts");
   323	                return (-1);
   324	        }
   325	
   326	        if (req->req_body_status == BS_CACHED) {
   327	                AZ(ObjGetU64(req->wrk, req->body_oc, OA_LEN, &u));
   328	                return (u);
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        if (req->req_body_status->avail <= 0)
   332	                return (req->req_body_status->avail);
   333	
   334	        if (req->htc->content_length > maxsize) {
   335	                req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
   336	                (void)VFP_Error(req->vfc, "Request body too big to cache");
   337	                return (-1);
   338	        }
   339	
   340	        return (vrb_pull(req, maxsize, NULL, NULL));
   341	}
   342

    50	sub vcl_req_host {
    51	        if (req.http.host ~ "[[:upper:]]") {
    52	                set req.http.host = req.http.host.lower();
    53	        }
    54	        if (!req.http.host &&
    55	            req.esi_level == 0 &&
    56	            req.proto == "HTTP/1.1") {
    57	                # In HTTP/1.1, Host is required.
    58	                return (synth(400));
    59	        }
    60	}
    61	
    62	sub vcl_req_method {
    63	        if (req.method == "PRI") {
    64	                # This will never happen in properly formed traffic.
    65	                return (synth(405));
    66	        }
    67	        if (req.method != "GET" &&
    68	            req.method != "HEAD" &&
    69	            req.method != "PUT" &&
    70	            req.method != "POST" &&
    71	            req.method != "TRACE" &&
    72	            req.method != "OPTIONS" &&
    73	            req.method != "DELETE" &&
    74	            req.method != "PATCH") {
    75	                # Non-RFC2616 or CONNECT which is weird.
    76	                return (pipe);
    77	        }
    78	        if (req.method != "GET" && req.method != "HEAD") {
    79	                # We only deal with GET and HEAD by default.
    80	                return (pass);
    81	        }
    82	}
    83	
    84	sub vcl_req_authorization {
    85	        if (req.http.Authorization) {
    86	                # Not cacheable by default.
    87	                return (pass);
    88	        }
    89	}
    90

    92	        if (req.http.Cookie) {
    93	                # Risky to cache by default.
    94	                return (pass);
    95	        }
    96	}

   237	            (!beresp.http.Surrogate-Control &&
   238	              beresp.http.Cache-Control ~ "(?i:no-cache|no-store|private)")) {
   239	                call vcl_beresp_hitmiss;
   240	        }
   241	}

   245	                call vcl_beresp_hitmiss;
   246	        }
   247	}
   248	
   249	sub vcl_beresp_range {
   250	        if (beresp.status != 206 && beresp.status != 416) {
   251	                # Content-Range has no meaning for these status codes
   252	                # Ref: https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110.html#section-14.4
   253	                unset beresp.http.Content-Range;
   254	        }
   255	}
   256	
   257	sub vcl_beresp_hitmiss {
   258	        set beresp.ttl = param.uncacheable_ttl;
   259	        set beresp.uncacheable = true;
   260	        return (deliver);
   261	}
   262	
   263	sub vcl_backend_error {
   264	        call vcl_builtin_backend_error;
   265	        return (deliver);
   266	}
   267	
   268	sub vcl_builtin_backend_error {
   269	        set beresp.http.Content-Type = "text/html; charset=utf-8";
   270	        set beresp.http.Retry-After = "5";
   271	        set beresp.body = {"<!DOCTYPE html>
   272	<html>
   273	  <head>
   274	    <title>"} + beresp.status + " " + beresp.reason + {"</title>
   275	  </head>
   276	  <body>
   277	    <h1>Error "} + beresp.status + " " + beresp.reason + {"</h1>
   278	    <p>"} + beresp.reason + {"</p>
   279	    <h3>Guru Meditation:</h3>
   280	    <p>XID: "} + bereq.xid + {"</p>
   281	    <hr>
   282	    <p>Varnish cache server</p>
   283	  </body>
   284	</html>
   285	"};
   286	}

   289	# Housekeeping
   290	
   291	sub vcl_init {
   292	        return (ok);
   293	}
   294	
   295	sub vcl_fini {
   296	        return (ok);
   297	}

    31	 * This file contains the two central state machine for pushing HTTP1
    32	 * sessions through their states.
    33	 *
    34	 */
    35	
    36	#include "config.h"
    37	
    38	#include <stdio.h>
    39	#include <stdlib.h>
    40	
    41	#include "cache/cache_varnishd.h"
    42	#include "cache/cache_objhead.h"

    47	
    48	static const char H1NEWREQ[] = "HTTP1::NewReq";
    49	static const char H1PROC[] = "HTTP1::Proc";
    50	static const char H1CLEANUP[] = "HTTP1::Cleanup";
    51	
    52	static void HTTP1_Session(struct worker *, struct req *);
    53	
    54	static void
    55	http1_setstate(const struct sess *sp, const char *s)
    56	{
    57	        uintptr_t p;
    58	
    59	        p = (uintptr_t)s;
    60	        AZ(SES_Set_proto_priv(sp, &p));
    61	}
    62	
    63	static const char *
    64	http1_getstate(const struct sess *sp)
    65	{
    66	        uintptr_t *p;
    67	
    68	        AZ(SES_Get_proto_priv(sp, &p));
    69	        return ((const char *)*p);
    70	}
    71	
    72	/*--------------------------------------------------------------------
    73	 * Call protocol for this request
    74	 */
    75	
    76	static void v_matchproto_(task_func_t)
    77	http1_req(struct worker *wrk, void *arg)
    78	{
    79	        struct req *req;
    80	
    81	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(wrk, WORKER_MAGIC);
    82	        CAST_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, arg, REQ_MAGIC);
    83	
    84	        THR_SetRequest(req);
    85	        assert(!WS_IsReserved(wrk->aws));
    86	        HTTP1_Session(wrk, req);
    87	        WS_Assert(wrk->aws);
    88	        THR_SetRequest(NULL);
    89	}

   237	static inline void
   238	http1_abort(struct req *req, uint16_t status)
   239	{
   240	        assert(req->doclose != SC_NULL);
   241	        assert(status >= 400);
   242	        (void)http1_minimal_response(req, status);
   243	}
   244	
   245	static int
   246	http1_dissect(struct worker *wrk, struct req *req)
   247	{
   248	
   249	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(wrk, WORKER_MAGIC);
   250	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
   251	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req->transport, TRANSPORT_MAGIC);
   252	
   253	        /* Allocate a new vxid now that we know we'll need it. */
   254	        assert(IS_NO_VXID(req->vsl->wid));
   255	        req->vsl->wid = VXID_Get(wrk, VSL_CLIENTMARKER);
   256	
   257	        VSLb(req->vsl, SLT_Begin, "req %ju rxreq", VXID(req->sp->vxid));
   258	        VSL(SLT_Link, req->sp->vxid, "req %ju rxreq", VXID(req->vsl->wid));
   259	        AZ(isnan(req->t_first)); /* First byte timestamp set by http1_wait */
   260	        AZ(isnan(req->t_req));   /* Complete req rcvd set by http1_wait */
   261	        req->t_prev = req->t_first;
   262	        VSLb_ts_req(req, "Start", req->t_first);
   263	        VSLb_ts_req(req, "Req", req->t_req);
   264	
   265	        HTTP_Setup(req->http, req->ws, req->vsl, SLT_ReqMethod);
   266	        req->err_code = HTTP1_DissectRequest(req->htc, req->http);
   267	
   268	        /* If we could not even parse the request, just close */
   269	        if (req->err_code != 0) {
   270	                VSLb(req->vsl, SLT_HttpGarbage, "%.*s",
   271	                    (int)(req->htc->rxbuf_e - req->htc->rxbuf_b),
   272	                    req->htc->rxbuf_b);
   273	                wrk->stats->client_req_400++;
   274	
   275	                (void)Req_LogStart(wrk, req);
   276	
   277	                req->doclose = SC_RX_JUNK;
   278	                http1_abort(req, 400);
   279	                return (-1);
   280	        }
   281	
   282	        AZ(req->req_body_status);
   283	        req->req_body_status = req->htc->body_status;
   284	        return (0);
   285	}

   291	HTTP1_Session(struct worker *wrk, struct req *req)
   292	{
   293	        enum htc_status_e hs;
   294	        struct sess *sp;
   295	        const char *st;
   296	        int i;
   297	
   298	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(wrk, WORKER_MAGIC);
   299	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
   300	        sp = req->sp;
   301	        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(sp, SESS_MAGIC);
   302	
   303	        /*
   304	         * Whenever we come in from the acceptor or waiter, we need to set
   305	         * blocking mode.  It would be simpler to do this in the acceptor
   306	         * or waiter, but we'd rather do the syscall in the worker thread.
   307	         */
   308	        if (http1_getstate(sp) == H1NEWREQ)
   309	                VTCP_blocking(sp->fd);
   310	        req->transport = XPORT_ByNumber(sp->sattr[SA_TRANSPORT]);
   311	
   312	        while (1) {
   313	                st = http1_getstate(sp);
   314	                if (st == H1NEWREQ) {
   315	                        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req->transport, TRANSPORT_MAGIC);
   316	                        assert(isnan(req->t_prev));
   317	                        assert(isnan(req->t_req));
   318	                        AZ(req->vcl);
   319	                        AZ(req->esi_level);
   320	                        AN(WS_Reservation(req->htc->ws));
   321	
   322	                        hs = HTC_RxStuff(req->htc, HTTP1_Complete,
   323	                            &req->t_first, &req->t_req,
   324	                            sp->t_idle + SESS_TMO(sp, timeout_linger),
   325	                            sp->t_idle + SESS_TMO(sp, timeout_idle),
   326	                            NAN,
   327	                            cache_param->http_req_size);
   328	                        assert(!WS_IsReserved(req->htc->ws));
   329	                        if (hs < HTC_S_EMPTY) {
   330	                                if (hs == HTC_S_OVERFLOW && cache_param->http_req_overflow_status != 0) {
   331	                                        (void)req->transport->minimal_response(req,
   332	                                            cache_param->http_req_overflow_status);
   333	                                }
   334	                                req->acct.req_hdrbytes +=
   335	                                    req->htc->rxbuf_e - req->htc->rxbuf_b;
   336	                                Req_AcctLogCharge(wrk->stats, req);
   337	                                Req_Release(req);
   338	                                SES_DeleteHS(sp, hs, NAN);
   339	                                return;
   340	                        }
   341	                        if (hs == HTC_S_IDLE) {
   342	                                wrk->stats->sess_herd++;
   343	                                Req_Release(req);
   344	                                SES_Wait(sp, &HTTP1_transport);
   345	                                return;
   346	                        }
   347	                        if (hs != HTC_S_COMPLETE)
   348	                                WRONG("htc_status (nonbad)");
   349

   351	                                if (!FEATURE(FEATURE_HTTP2)) {
   352	                                        SES_Close(req->sp, SC_REQ_HTTP20);
   353	                                        assert(!WS_IsReserved(req->ws));
   354	                                        assert(!WS_IsReserved(wrk->aws));
   355	                                        http1_setstate(sp, H1CLEANUP);
   356	                                        continue;
   357	                                }
   358	                                http1_setstate(sp, NULL);
   359	                                H2_PU_Sess(wrk, sp, req);
   360	                                return;
   361	                        }
   362	
   363	                        i = http1_dissect(wrk, req);
   364	                        req->acct.req_hdrbytes +=
   365	                            req->htc->rxbuf_e - req->htc->rxbuf_b;
   366	                        if (i) {
   367	                                assert(req->doclose != SC_NULL);
   368	                                SES_Close(req->sp, req->doclose);
   369	                                assert(!WS_IsReserved(req->ws));
   370	                                assert(!WS_IsReserved(wrk->aws));
   371	                                http1_setstate(sp, H1CLEANUP);
   372	                                continue;

So I see the issue now. There are two places where BS_ERROR is checked:
1. Early in `cnt_recv` before calling VCL - it sets `SC_OVERLOAD`
2. Later in `cnt_recv` after VCL (for cached body attempts) - it sets `SC_RX_BODY`

The problem is that when `REQ_FSM_DONE` is returned and `doclose` is set, the session is just closed without sending a proper error response. The test is showing 503 errors, which suggests that maybe something else is happening or there's some default behavior.

Let me understand what SC codes mean and what happens when a session closes without a response being sent:

static void v_matchproto_(vtr_req_body_t)
http1_req_body(struct req *req)
{

	CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
	if (V1F_Setup_Fetch(req->vfc, req->htc) != 0)
		req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR;
}

http1_sess_panic(struct vsb *vsb, const struct sess *sp)
{

	VSB_printf(vsb, "state = %s\n", http1_getstate(sp));
}

static inline void
http1_abort(struct req *req, uint16_t status)
{
	assert(req->doclose != SC_NULL);
	assert(status >= 400);
	(void)http1_minimal_response(req, status);
}

/**********************************************************************
 */

void
VFP_Setup(struct vfp_ctx *vc, struct worker *wrk)
{

	INIT_OBJ(vc, VFP_CTX_MAGIC);
	VTAILQ_INIT(&vc->vfp);
	vc->wrk = wrk;
}

Actually, wait. Let me re-examine the problem. The VFP_Error function logs the error message, but where does the 503 response get sent? Let me trace through this more carefully.

Looking back at the code flow:
1. `http1_req_body` is called, which calls `V1F_Setup_Fetch`
2. If that fails, it sets `req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR`
3. In `cnt_recv`, if `req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR`, it either sets `doclose = SC_OVERLOAD` (early check) or `doclose = SC_RX_BODY` (later check) and returns `REQ_FSM_DONE`
4. The session is then closed without sending a proper error response

So the problem is that no HTTP error response is being sent at all when the chunked encoding is bad. The test expects 503, but according to the PR description, the test should expect 400.

Wait, let me re-read the PR description. It says "The test for VSV16 shows that malformed chunked responses cause a 503 error, which is clearly wrong." But the test is testing malformed chunked *requests* (POST from client), not responses. Let me look at the test file again more carefully:

str_replace_editor create /testbed/reproduce_issue.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Script to reproduce the chunked encoding issue.
This script verifies that bad chunked encoding from client results in 503 instead of 400.
"""

import socket
import time

def send_bad_chunked_request(host='"'"'127.0.0.1'"'"', port=8080):
    """Send a POST request with bad chunked encoding."""
    try:
        # Create socket
        s = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
        s.settimeout(5)
        s.connect((host, port))
        
        # Send request with bad chunked encoding
        # Sending "1\r\n" means 1 byte follows, but we send much more
        request = (
            b"POST / HTTP/1.1\r\n"
            b"Host: localhost\r\n"
            b"Transfer-Encoding: chunked\r\n"
            b"\r\n"
            b"1\r\n"
            b"This is more than one byte of data\r\n"
            b"0\r\n"
            b"\r\n"
        )
        
        print(f"Sending bad chunked request to {host}:{port}")
        print(f"Request:\n{request.decode('"'"'latin1'"'"')}")
        
        s.sendall(request)
        
        # Read response
        response = b""
        while True:
            try:
                chunk = s.recv(4096)
                if not chunk:
                    break
                response += chunk
            except socket.timeout:
                break
        
        s.close()
        
        # Parse response
        response_str = response.decode('"'"'latin1'"'"', errors='"'"'replace'"'"')
        print(f"\nResponse:\n{response_str}")
        
        # Extract status code
        if response_str:
            first_line = response_str.split('"'"'\r\n'"'"')[0]
            print(f"\nFirst line: {first_line}")
            if '"'"'HTTP'"'"' in first_line:
                parts = first_line.split()
                if len(parts) >= 2:
                    status_code = parts[1]
                    print(f"Status code: {status_code}")
                    return status_code
        
        print("No valid HTTP response received")
        return None
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")
        return None

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("This script needs a running Varnish instance on port 8080")
    print("Run the test with: make -C bin/varnishtest check-TESTS TESTS=tests/f00016.vtc")
    print("\nThe current behavior returns 503, but it should return 400")
    print("because the error is from the client, not a backend failure.")

1. When a client sends a POST with bad chunked encoding, Varnish should return 400 Bad Request
2. When a backend sends a response with bad chunked encoding, Varnish should return 503 Service Unavailable

This makes sense! 400 means "client error", 503 means "backend error".

So I need to modify the code to:
1. Detect whether the chunked encoding error is from processing a client request body or a backend response body
2. Return different error codes accordingly

Now, the question is: where should I send the 400 error response when the client request body has bad chunked encoding?

Looking at the code flow again:
1. `http1_req_body` sets `req->req_body_status = BS_ERROR` when `V1F_Setup_Fetch` fails
2. In `cnt_recv`, we check for `BS_ERROR` and just set `doclose` and return `REQ_FSM_DONE`
3. No error response is sent

The fix should be to send an error response before setting doclose. Let me look at how other 400 errors are handled:

	HTTP_Clone(req->http0, req->http);	// For ESI & restart
	req->req_step = R_STP_RECV;
	return (REQ_FSM_MORE);
}

So `VFP_Suck` is called from `vrb_pull` in `cache_req_body.c`. When `VFP_Suck` returns `VFP_ERROR`, the `vfc->failed` flag is set and the body status becomes `BS_ERROR`.

Now the key question is: at what point should we send the 400 response? Looking at the cnt_recv code:

```c
if (req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR) {
    req->doclose = SC_OVERLOAD;  // or SC_RX_BODY
    return (REQ_FSM_DONE);
}
```

This just closes the connection without sending a response. We need to send a 400 response here.

But there's a problem: we need to differentiate between:
1. Client request body errors (should return 400)
2. Errors that happen during backend fetching (should return 503)

Looking at the code again, when we're in `cnt_recv` and checking `req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR`, we're definitely dealing with client request body errors, not backend errors. Backend errors would be in a different context (busyobj, not req).

So the fix is simple: in `cnt_recv`, when `req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR`, we should send a 400 response before closing.

But wait, I need to check if the response headers have already been sent. Let me look at the state machine more carefully. At the point where we check `req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR` in `cnt_recv`, have we sent any response yet? No, because `cnt_recv` is early in the request processing - we haven't even called the VCL yet.

OK so here's my plan:
1. In `cnt_recv`, when `req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR`, send a 400 response using `req->transport->minimal_response(req, 400)`
2. Update the statistics counter appropriately
3. Set `doclose` appropriately

+        status = http_GetStatus(req->resp);

+        if (req->boc != NULL || (req->objcore->flags & (OC_F_FAILED)))
+                req->resp_len = clval;
+        else
+                req->resp_len = ObjGetLen(req->wrk, req->objcore);
+
+        if (head || status < 200 || status == 204 || status == 304) {
+                // rfc7230,l,1748,1752
+                sendbody = 0;
+        } else {
+                sendbody = 1;
+        }
+
+        VDP_Init(req->vdc, req->wrk, req->vsl, req, NULL, &req->resp_len);
+        if (req->vdp_filter_list == NULL)
+                req->vdp_filter_list = resp_Get_Filter_List(req);

+            VCL_StackVDP(req->vdc, req->vcl, req->vdp_filter_list, req, NULL)) {
+                VSLb(req->vsl, SLT_Error, "Failure to push processors");
+                req->doclose = SC_OVERLOAD;
+                req->acct.resp_bodybytes +=
+                        VDP_Close(req->vdc, req->objcore, req->boc);
+        } else {
+                if (status < 200 || status == 204) {
+                        // rfc7230,l,1691,1695
+                        http_Unset(req->resp, H_Content_Length);
+                } else if (status == 304) {
+                        // rfc7230,l,1675,1677
+                        http_Unset(req->resp, H_Content_Length);
+                } else if (clval >= 0 && clval == req->resp_len) {
+                        /* Reuse C-L header */
+                } else if (head && req->objcore->flags & OC_F_HFM) {
+                        /*
+                         * Don't touch C-L header (debatable)
+                         *
+                         * The only way to do it correctly would be to GET
+                         * to the backend, and discard the body once the
+                         * filters have had a chance to chew on it, but that
+                         * would negate the "pass for huge objects" use case.
+                         */
+                } else {
+                        http_Unset(req->resp, H_Content_Length);
+                        if (req->resp_len >= 0)
+                                http_PrintfHeader(req->resp,
+                                    "Content-Length: %jd", req->resp_len);
+                }
+                if (req->resp_len == 0)
+                        sendbody = 0;
+                dnxt = req->transport->deliver(req, sendbody);
+                if (dnxt == VTR_D_DISEMBARK)
+                        nxt = REQ_FSM_DISEMBARK;
+                else
+                        assert(dnxt == VTR_D_DONE);
+        }
+        return (nxt);

+                CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(wrk->wpriv, WORKER_PRIV_MAGIC);
+                CHECK_OBJ_ORNULL(wrk->wpriv->nobjhead, OBJHEAD_MAGIC);
+                CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req, REQ_MAGIC);
+                CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(req->doclose, STREAM_CLOSE_MAGIC);
+
+                AN(req->req_step);
+                AN(req->req_step->name);
+                AN(req->req_step->func);
+                if (DO_DEBUG(DBG_REQ_STATE))
+                        cnt_diag(req, req->req_step->name);
+                nxt = req->req_step->func(wrk, req);
+                CHECK_OBJ_ORNULL(wrk->wpriv->nobjhead, OBJHEAD_MAGIC);
+        }
+        wrk->vsl = NULL;
+        if (nxt == REQ_FSM_DONE) {
+                INIT_OBJ(ctx, VRT_CTX_MAGIC);
+                VCL_Req2Ctx(ctx, req);
+                if (IS_TOPREQ(req)) {
+                        VCL_TaskLeave(ctx, req->top->privs);
+                        if (req->top->vcl0 != NULL)
+                                VCL_Recache(wrk, &req->top->vcl0);
+                }
+                VCL_TaskLeave(ctx, req->privs);
+                assert(!IS_NO_VXID(req->vsl->wid));
+                VRB_Free(req);
+                VRT_Assign_Backend(&req->director_hint, NULL);
+                req->wrk = NULL;
+        }
+        assert(nxt == REQ_FSM_DISEMBARK || !WS_IsReserved(req->ws));
+        return (nxt);
 }

+        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(wrk, WORKER_MAGIC);
+        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(bo, BUSYOBJ_MAGIC);
+        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(bo->htc, HTTP_CONN_MAGIC);
+        CHECK_OBJ_ORNULL(bo->req, REQ_MAGIC);
+        AN(ctr_hdrbytes);
+        AN(ctr_bodybytes);

+        htc = bo->htc;
+        assert(*htc->rfd > 0);
+        hp = bo->bereq;
+
+        if (bo->bereq_body != NULL)
+                cl = ObjGetLen(wrk, bo->bereq_body);
+        else if (bo->req != NULL && !bo->req->req_body_status->length_known)
+                cl = -1;
+        else if (bo->req != NULL) {
+                cl = http_GetContentLength(bo->req->http);
+                if (cl < 0)
+                        cl = 0;
+        }
+        else
+                cl = 0;
+
+        VDP_Init(vdc, wrk, bo->vsl, NULL, bo, &cl);
+        if (bo->vdp_filter_list != NULL &&
+            VCL_StackVDP(vdc, bo->vcl, bo->vdp_filter_list, NULL, bo))
+                err = "Failure to push processors";
+        else if ((v1l = V1L_Open(wrk->aws, htc->rfd, bo->vsl, nan(""), 0)) == NULL) {
+                /*      ^^^^^^^^
+                 * XXX: need a send_timeout for the backend side
+                 * XXX: use cache_param->http1_iovs ?
+                 */
+                err = "Failure to open V1L (workspace_thread overflow)";
+        }
+        else if (v1f_stackv1l(vdc, bo, v1l))
+                err = "Failure to push V1L";
+
+        if (err != NULL) {
+                if (v1l != NULL)
+                        (void) V1L_Close(&v1l, &bytes);
+                if (VALID_OBJ(vdc, VDP_CTX_MAGIC))
+                        (void) VDP_Close(vdc, NULL, NULL);
+                VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "%s", err);
+                VSLb_ts_busyobj(bo, "Bereq", W_TIM_real(wrk));
+                htc->doclose = SC_OVERLOAD;
+                return (-1);
+        }
+
+
+        assert(cl >= -1);
+        if (cl < 0)
+                http_PrintfHeader(hp, "Transfer-Encoding: chunked");
+
+        VTCP_blocking(*htc->rfd);       /* XXX: we should timeout instead */
+        hdrbytes = HTTP1_Write(v1l, hp, HTTP1_Req);
+
+        /* Deal with any message-body the request might (still) have */
+        i = 0;
+
+        if (bo->bereq_body != NULL) {
+                AZ(bo->req);
+                assert(cl >= 0);
+                (void)ObjIterate(bo->wrk, bo->bereq_body,
+                    vdc, VDP_ObjIterate, 0);
+        } else if (bo->req != NULL &&
+            bo->req->req_body_status != BS_NONE) {
+                if (cl < 0)
+                        V1L_Chunked(v1l);
+                i = VRB_Iterate(wrk, bo->vsl, bo->req, VDP_ObjIterate, vdc);
+
+                if (bo->req->req_body_status != BS_CACHED)
+                        bo->no_retry = "req.body not cached";
+
+                if (bo->req->req_body_status == BS_ERROR) {
+                        /*
+                         * XXX: (#2332) We should test to see if the backend
+                         * XXX: sent us some headers explaining why.
+                         * XXX: This is hard because of the mistaken API split
+                         * XXX: between cache_backend.c and V1F, and therefore
+                         * XXX: Parked in this comment, pending renovation of
+                         * XXX: the VDI/backend-protocol API to allow non-H1
+                         * XXX: backends.
+                         */
+                        assert(i < 0);
+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError,
+                            "req.body read error: %d (%s)",
+                            errno, VAS_errtxt(errno));
+                        bo->req->doclose = SC_RX_BODY;
+                        bo->err_code = 400;
+                }
+                if (cl < 0)
+                        V1L_EndChunk(v1l);
+        }
+
+        sc = V1L_Close(&v1l, &bytes);
+        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(sc, STREAM_CLOSE_MAGIC);
+
+        /* Bytes accounting */
+        *ctr_hdrbytes += hdrbytes;
+        *ctr_bodybytes += VDP_Close(vdc, NULL, NULL);
+
+        if (sc == SC_NULL && i < 0)
+                sc = SC_TX_ERROR;
+
+        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(sc, STREAM_CLOSE_MAGIC);
+        if (sc != SC_NULL) {
+                VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError,
+                    "backend write error: %d (%s) (%s)",
+                    errno, VAS_errtxt(errno), sc->desc);
+                VSLb_ts_busyobj(bo, "Bereq", W_TIM_real(wrk));
+                htc->doclose = sc;
+                return (-1);
+        }
+        CHECK_OBJ_NOTNULL(sc, STREAM_CLOSE_MAGIC);
+        VSLb_ts_busyobj(bo, "Bereq", W_TIM_real(wrk));
+        return (0);
 }

+
+        /* Receive response */
+

+        hs = HTC_RxStuff(htc, HTTP1_Complete, NULL, NULL,
+            t, NAN, htc->between_bytes_timeout, cache_param->http_resp_size);
+        if (hs != HTC_S_COMPLETE) {
+                bo->acct.beresp_hdrbytes +=

+                        htc->doclose = SC_RX_JUNK;
+                        break;
+                case HTC_S_CLOSE:
+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "backend closed");
+                        htc->doclose = SC_RESP_CLOSE;
+                        break;
+                case HTC_S_TIMEOUT:
+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "timeout");
+                        htc->doclose = SC_RX_TIMEOUT;
+                        break;
+                case HTC_S_OVERFLOW:
+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "overflow");
+                        htc->doclose = SC_RX_OVERFLOW;
+                        break;
+                case HTC_S_IDLE:
+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "first byte timeout");
+                        htc->doclose = SC_RX_TIMEOUT;
+                        break;

+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "HTC %s (%s)",
+                             name, desc);
+                        htc->doclose = SC_RX_BAD;
+                        break;
+                }
+                return (htc->rxbuf_e == htc->rxbuf_b ? 1 : -1);
+        }
+        VTCP_set_read_timeout(*htc->rfd, htc->between_bytes_timeout);
+
+        hp = bo->beresp;
+
+        i = HTTP1_DissectResponse(htc, hp, bo->bereq);
+        bo->acct.beresp_hdrbytes += htc->rxbuf_e - htc->rxbuf_b;
+        if (i) {
+                VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "http format error");
+                htc->doclose = SC_RX_JUNK;
+                return (-1);
+        }
+
+        htc->doclose = http_DoConnection(hp, SC_RESP_CLOSE);
+
+        /*
+         * Figure out how the fetch is supposed to happen, before the
+         * headers are adulterated by VCL
+         */
+        if (http_method_eq(http_GetMethod(bo->bereq), HEAD)) {

+                 * A HEAD request can never have a body in the reply,
+                 * no matter what the headers might say.
+                 * [RFC7231 4.3.2 p25]
+                 */
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_head++;
+                bo->htc->body_status = BS_NONE;
+        } else if (http_GetStatus(bo->beresp) <= 199) {
+                /*
+                 * 1xx responses never have a body.
+                 * [RFC7230 3.3.2 p31]
+                 * ... but we should never see them.
+                 */
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_1xx++;
+                bo->htc->body_status = BS_ERROR;
+        } else if (http_IsStatus(bo->beresp, 204)) {
+                /*
+                 * 204 is "No Content", obviously don't expect a body.
+                 * [RFC7230 3.3.1 p29 and 3.3.2 p31]
+                 */
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_204++;
+                if ((http_GetHdr(bo->beresp, H_Content_Length, NULL) &&
+                    bo->htc->content_length != 0) ||
+                    http_GetHdr(bo->beresp, H_Transfer_Encoding, NULL))
+                        bo->htc->body_status = BS_ERROR;
+                else
+                        bo->htc->body_status = BS_NONE;
+        } else if (http_IsStatus(bo->beresp, 304)) {
+                /*
+                 * 304 is "Not Modified" it has no body.
+                 * [RFC7230 3.3 p28]
+                 */
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_304++;
+                bo->htc->body_status = BS_NONE;
+        } else if (bo->htc->body_status == BS_CHUNKED) {
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_chunked++;
+        } else if (bo->htc->body_status == BS_LENGTH) {
+                assert(bo->htc->content_length > 0);
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_length++;
+        } else if (bo->htc->body_status == BS_EOF) {
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_eof++;
+        } else if (bo->htc->body_status == BS_ERROR) {
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_bad++;
+        } else if (bo->htc->body_status == BS_NONE) {
+                bo->wrk->stats->fetch_none++;
+        } else {
+                WRONG("wrong bodystatus");
+        }
+
+        assert(bo->vfc->resp == bo->beresp);
+        if (bo->htc->body_status != BS_NONE &&
+            bo->htc->body_status != BS_ERROR)
+                if (V1F_Setup_Fetch(bo->vfc, bo->htc)) {
+                        VSLb(bo->vsl, SLT_FetchError, "overflow");
+                        htc->doclose = SC_RX_OVERFLOW;
+                        return (-1);
+                }
+
+        return (0);
 }

diff --git a/reproduce_issue.py b/reproduce_issue.py
new file mode 100755
index 000000000..6b80e6666
--- /dev/null
+++ b/reproduce_issue.py
@@ -0,0 +1,75 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Script to reproduce the chunked encoding issue.
+This script verifies that bad chunked encoding from client results in 503 instead of 400.
+"""
+
+import socket
+import time
+
+def send_bad_chunked_request(host='127.0.0.1', port=8080):
+    """Send a POST request with bad chunked encoding."""
+    try:
+        # Create socket
+        s = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
+        s.settimeout(5)
+        s.connect((host, port))
+        
+        # Send request with bad chunked encoding
+        # Sending "1\r\n" means 1 byte follows, but we send much more
+        request = (
+            b"POST / HTTP/1.1\r\n"
+            b"Host: localhost\r\n"
+            b"Transfer-Encoding: chunked\r\n"
+            b"\r\n"
+            b"1\r\n"
+            b"This is more than one byte of data\r\n"
+            b"0\r\n"
+            b"\r\n"
+        )
+        
+        print(f"Sending bad chunked request to {host}:{port}")
+        print(f"Request:\n{request.decode('latin1')}")
+        
+        s.sendall(request)
+        
+        # Read response
+        response = b""
+        while True:
+            try:
+                chunk = s.recv(4096)
+                if not chunk:
+                    break
+                response += chunk
+            except socket.timeout:
+                break
+        
+        s.close()
+        
+        # Parse response
+        response_str = response.decode('latin1', errors='replace')
+        print(f"\nResponse:\n{response_str}")
+        
+        # Extract status code
+        if response_str:
+            first_line = response_str.split('\r\n')[0]
+            print(f"\nFirst line: {first_line}")
+            if 'HTTP' in first_line:
+                parts = first_line.split()
+                if len(parts) >= 2:
+                    status_code = parts[1]
+                    print(f"Status code: {status_code}")
+                    return status_code
+        
+        print("No valid HTTP response received")
+        return None
+        
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"Error: {e}")
+        return None
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    print("This script needs a running Varnish instance on port 8080")
+    print("Run the test with: make -C bin/varnishtest check-TESTS TESTS=tests/f00016.vtc")
+    print("\nThe current behavior returns 503, but it should return 400")
+    print("because the error is from the client, not a backend failure.")
